|              |                                             |             * Storm Control limits the rate on rx ports through        |                 |                         |
|              |                                             | changes in tx port's speeds.                                           |                 |                         |

+------+------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| Step | Step Description                                                       |

+------+------------------------------------------------------------------------+

+------+------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| 3    | Create VLAN filtering aware bridge entity and set link up on it.       |
|      | Enslave all participant ports to the bridge                            |
+------+------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| 4    | Add each pair of ports to a different VLAN id                          |
+------+------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| 5    | Wait till all ports get up                                             |
+------+------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| 6    | Set up broadcast, multicast and unknown unicast streams on ixia tx     |
|      | port                                                                   |
+------+------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| 7    | Set storm control rate limit for all types of traffic on all ports     |
+------+------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| 8    | Transmit traffic of all streams simultaneously                         |
+------+------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| 9    | Verify rx rate on rx port is as expected - rate is limited by storm    |
|      | control                                                                |
+------+------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| 10   | Change ports speed to 100Mb full duplex                                |
+------+------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| 11   | Verify mode on ports                                                   |
+------+------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| 12   | Transmit traffic again                                                 |
+------+------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| 13   | Verify rate on rx port is as expected - rate is limited by storm       |

+------+------------------------------------------------------------------------+

+------+------------------------------------------------------------------------+
